\subsection{Detailed Description}
Official documentation for S\+DL configuration variables

This file contains functions to set and get configuration hints, as well as listing each of them alphabetically.

The convention for naming hints is S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+X, where \char`\"{}\+S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+X\char`\"{} is the environment variable that can be used to override the default.

In general these hints are just that -\/ they may or may not be supported or applicable on any given platform, but they provide a way for an application or user to give the library a hint as to how they would like the library to work.

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+L\+E\+R\+O\+M\+E\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+S\+\_\+\+J\+O\+Y\+S\+T\+I\+CK}{SDL\_HINT\_ACCELEROMETER\_AS\_JOYSTICK}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+L\+E\+R\+O\+M\+E\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+S\+\_\+\+J\+O\+Y\+S\+T\+I\+CK~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+L\+E\+R\+O\+M\+E\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+S\+\_\+\+J\+O\+Y\+S\+T\+I\+CK\char`\"{}}



A variable controlling whether the Android / i\+OS built-\/in accelerometer should be listed as a joystick device. 

This variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ The accelerometer is not listed as a joystick \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ The accelerometer is available as a 3 axis joystick (the default). \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_ac0deec953ae4635131cbe321192236ff}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_ac0deec953ae4635131cbe321192236ff}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+O\+P\+M\+O\+ST@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+O\+P\+M\+O\+ST}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+O\+P\+M\+O\+ST@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+O\+P\+M\+O\+ST}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+O\+P\+M\+O\+ST}{SDL\_HINT\_ALLOW\_TOPMOST}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+O\+P\+M\+O\+ST~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+T\+O\+P\+M\+O\+ST\char`\"{}}



If set to \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} then never set the top most bit on a S\+DL Window, even if the video mode expects it. This is a debugging aid for developers and not expected to be used by end users. The default is \char`\"{}1\char`\"{}. 

This variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ don\textquotesingle{}t allow topmost \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ allow topmost \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a83f55aca7bd64c9157f00ad356bda81e}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a83f55aca7bd64c9157f00ad356bda81e}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}{SDL\_HINT\_ANDROID\_APK\_EXPANSION\_MAIN\_FILE\_VERSION}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON\char`\"{}}



Android A\+PK expansion main file version. Should be a string number like \char`\"{}1\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}2\char`\"{} etc. 

Must be set together with S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON.

If both hints were set then \mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__rwops_8h_aef7e843c3486bd1770667a594aa0b439}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+R\+W\+From\+File()}} will look into expansion files after a given relative path was not found in the internal storage and assets.

By default this hint is not set and the A\+PK expansion files are not searched. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_ac2dce1bbb095169a9de048eeee233e2d}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_ac2dce1bbb095169a9de048eeee233e2d}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON}{SDL\_HINT\_ANDROID\_APK\_EXPANSION\_PATCH\_FILE\_VERSION}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+P\+A\+T\+C\+H\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON\char`\"{}}



Android A\+PK expansion patch file version. Should be a string number like \char`\"{}1\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}2\char`\"{} etc. 

Must be set together with S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+A\+P\+K\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+A\+N\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+M\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+V\+E\+R\+S\+I\+ON.

If both hints were set then \mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__rwops_8h_aef7e843c3486bd1770667a594aa0b439}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+R\+W\+From\+File()}} will look into expansion files after a given relative path was not found in the internal storage and assets.

By default this hint is not set and the A\+PK expansion files are not searched. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a46ee702b1e7f6c0fd1a35e64a1e68fe6}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a46ee702b1e7f6c0fd1a35e64a1e68fe6}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+T\+O\+U\+CH@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+T\+O\+U\+CH}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+T\+O\+U\+CH@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+T\+O\+U\+CH}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+T\+O\+U\+CH}{SDL\_HINT\_ANDROID\_SEPARATE\_MOUSE\_AND\_TOUCH}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+T\+O\+U\+CH~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+R\+O\+I\+D\+\_\+\+S\+E\+P\+A\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+T\+O\+U\+CH\char`\"{}}



A variable to control whether mouse and touch events are to be treated together or separately. 

The variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ Mouse events will be handled as touch events, and touch will raise fake mouse events. This is the behaviour of S\+DL $<$= 2.\+0.\+3. (default) \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ Mouse events will be handled separately from pure touch events.

The value of this hint is used at runtime, so it can be changed at any time. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a0301d6377ef50a5a435653743d2771f4}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a0301d6377ef50a5a435653743d2771f4}}

\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+U\+I\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+U\+I\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+U\+I\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS}{SDL\_HINT\_APPLE\_TV\_CONTROLLER\_UI\_EVENTS}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+U\+I\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+U\+I\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS\char`\"{}}



A variable controlling whether controllers used with the Apple TV generate UI events. 

When UI events are generated by controller input, the app will be backgrounded when the Apple TV remote\textquotesingle{}s menu button is pressed, and when the pause or B buttons on gamepads are pressed.

More information about properly making use of controllers for the Apple TV can be found here\+: \href{https://developer.apple.com/tvos/human-interface-guidelines/remote-and-controllers/}{\tt https\+://developer.\+apple.\+com/tvos/human-\/interface-\/guidelines/remote-\/and-\/controllers/}

This variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ Controller input does not generate UI events (the default). \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ Controller input generates UI events. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a9b66ef93d2b547e671881bbfdf6c2ddc}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a9b66ef93d2b547e671881bbfdf6c2ddc}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+R\+O\+T\+A\+T\+I\+ON@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+R\+O\+T\+A\+T\+I\+ON}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+R\+O\+T\+A\+T\+I\+ON@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+R\+O\+T\+A\+T\+I\+ON}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+R\+O\+T\+A\+T\+I\+ON}{SDL\_HINT\_APPLE\_TV\_REMOTE\_ALLOW\_ROTATION}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+R\+O\+T\+A\+T\+I\+ON~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+A\+P\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+V\+\_\+\+R\+E\+M\+O\+T\+E\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+R\+O\+T\+A\+T\+I\+ON\char`\"{}}



A variable controlling whether the Apple TV remote\textquotesingle{}s joystick axes will automatically match the rotation of the remote. 

This variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ Remote orientation does not affect joystick axes (the default). \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ Joystick axes are based on the orientation of the remote. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_aadfee7d079b71eebc291fc42622ead38}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_aadfee7d079b71eebc291fc42622ead38}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+RY@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+RY}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+RY@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+RY}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+RY}{SDL\_HINT\_AUDIO\_CATEGORY}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+RY~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+C\+A\+T\+E\+G\+O\+RY\char`\"{}}



A variable controlling the audio category on i\+OS and Mac OS X. 

This variable can be set to the following values\+:

\char`\"{}ambient\char`\"{} -\/ Use the A\+V\+Audio\+Session\+Category\+Ambient audio category, will be muted by the phone mute switch (default) \char`\"{}playback\char`\"{} -\/ Use the A\+V\+Audio\+Session\+Category\+Playback category

For more information, see Apple\textquotesingle{}s documentation\+: \href{https://developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Audio/Conceptual/AudioSessionProgrammingGuide/AudioSessionCategoriesandModes/AudioSessionCategoriesandModes.html}{\tt https\+://developer.\+apple.\+com/library/content/documentation/\+Audio/\+Conceptual/\+Audio\+Session\+Programming\+Guide/\+Audio\+Session\+Categoriesand\+Modes/\+Audio\+Session\+Categoriesand\+Modes.\+html} \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_ac95cc95cd003647ccc6b1446a7e3c408}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_ac95cc95cd003647ccc6b1446a7e3c408}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}{SDL\_HINT\_AUDIO\_RESAMPLING\_MODE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+A\+U\+D\+I\+O\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE\char`\"{}}



A variable controlling speed/quality tradeoff of audio resampling. 

If available, S\+DL can use libsamplerate ( \href{http://www.mega-nerd.com/SRC/}{\tt http\+://www.\+mega-\/nerd.\+com/\+S\+R\+C/} ) to handle audio resampling. There are different resampling modes available that produce different levels of quality, using more C\+PU.

If this hint isn\textquotesingle{}t specified to a valid setting, or libsamplerate isn\textquotesingle{}t available, S\+DL will use the default, internal resampling algorithm.

Note that this is currently only applicable to resampling audio that is being written to a device for playback or audio being read from a device for capture. \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_s_d_l___audio_c_v_t}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Audio\+C\+VT}} always uses the default resampler (although this might change for S\+DL 2.\+1).

This hint is currently only checked at audio subsystem initialization.

This variable can be set to the following values\+:

\char`\"{}0\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}default\char`\"{} -\/ Use S\+DL\textquotesingle{}s internal resampling (Default when not set -\/ low quality, fast) \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}fast\char`\"{} -\/ Use fast, slightly higher quality resampling, if available \char`\"{}2\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}medium\char`\"{} -\/ Use medium quality resampling, if available \char`\"{}3\char`\"{} or \char`\"{}best\char`\"{} -\/ Use high quality resampling, if available \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a75c4ce4bba90833587eae21903d3d3fe}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a75c4ce4bba90833587eae21903d3d3fe}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+B\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+B\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+B\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+B\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+B\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT}{SDL\_HINT\_BMP\_SAVE\_LEGACY\_FORMAT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+B\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+B\+M\+P\+\_\+\+S\+A\+V\+E\+\_\+\+L\+E\+G\+A\+C\+Y\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+AT\char`\"{}}



Prevent S\+DL from using version 4 of the bitmap header when saving B\+M\+Ps. 

The bitmap header version 4 is required for proper alpha channel support and S\+DL will use it when required. Should this not be desired, this hint can force the use of the 40 byte header version which is supported everywhere.

The variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ Surfaces with a colorkey or an alpha channel are saved to a 32-\/bit B\+MP file with an alpha mask. S\+DL will use the bitmap header version 4 and set the alpha mask accordingly. \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ Surfaces with a colorkey or an alpha channel are saved to a 32-\/bit B\+MP file without an alpha mask. The alpha channel data will be in the file, but applications are going to ignore it.

The default value is \char`\"{}0\char`\"{}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a70b9664a38b946b73b669be38add94ef}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a70b9664a38b946b73b669be38add94ef}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+M\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+E\+N\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+E\+L\+E\+M\+E\+NT@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+M\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+E\+N\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+E\+L\+E\+M\+E\+NT}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+M\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+E\+N\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+E\+L\+E\+M\+E\+NT@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+M\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+E\+N\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+E\+L\+E\+M\+E\+NT}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+M\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+E\+N\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+E\+L\+E\+M\+E\+NT}{SDL\_HINT\_EMSCRIPTEN\_KEYBOARD\_ELEMENT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+E\+M\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+E\+N\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+E\+L\+E\+M\+E\+NT~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+E\+M\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+E\+N\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+R\+D\+\_\+\+E\+L\+E\+M\+E\+NT\char`\"{}}



override the binding element for keyboard inputs for Emscripten builds 

This hint only applies to the emscripten platform

The variable can be one of \char`\"{}\#window\char`\"{} -\/ The javascript window object (this is the default) \char`\"{}\#document\char`\"{} -\/ The javascript document object \char`\"{}\#screen\char`\"{} -\/ the javascript window.\+screen object \char`\"{}\#canvas\char`\"{} -\/ the Web\+GL canvas element any other string without a leading \# sign applies to the element on the page with that ID. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a4f14744afc8f84bf52e3bfaec2667824}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a4f14744afc8f84bf52e3bfaec2667824}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+L\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+ON@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+L\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+ON}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+L\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+ON@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+L\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+ON}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+L\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+ON}{SDL\_HINT\_FRAMEBUFFER\_ACCELERATION}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+L\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+ON~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+B\+U\+F\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+A\+C\+C\+E\+L\+E\+R\+A\+T\+I\+ON\char`\"{}}



A variable controlling how 3D acceleration is used to accelerate the S\+DL screen surface. 

S\+DL can try to accelerate the S\+DL screen surface by using streaming textures with a 3D rendering engine. This variable controls whether and how this is done.

This variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ Disable 3D acceleration \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ Enable 3D acceleration, using the default renderer. \char`\"{}\+X\char`\"{} -\/ Enable 3D acceleration, using X where X is one of the valid rendering drivers. (e.\+g. \char`\"{}direct3d\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}opengl\char`\"{}, etc.)

By default S\+DL tries to make a best guess for each platform whether to use acceleration or not. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_ad14dbbb2b528c47f178f3daf35d9136b}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_ad14dbbb2b528c47f178f3daf35d9136b}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+ES@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+ES}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+ES@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+ES}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+ES}{SDL\_HINT\_GAMECONTROLLER\_IGNORE\_DEVICES}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+ES~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+ES\char`\"{}}

\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+S\+\_\+\+E\+X\+C\+E\+PT@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+S\+\_\+\+E\+X\+C\+E\+PT}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+S\+\_\+\+E\+X\+C\+E\+PT@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+S\+\_\+\+E\+X\+C\+E\+PT}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+R\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+V\+I\+C\+E\+S\+\_\+\+E\+X\+C\+E\+PT}{SDL\_HINT\_GAMECONTROLLER\_IGNORE\_DEVICES\_EXCEPT}}

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+C\+O\+N\+F\+IG}{SDL\_HINT\_GAMECONTROLLERCONFIG}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+C\+O\+N\+F\+IG~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+C\+O\+N\+F\+IG\char`\"{}}



A variable that lets you manually hint extra gamecontroller db entries. 

The variable should be newline delimited rows of gamecontroller config data, see S\+D\+L\+\_\+gamecontroller.\+h

This hint must be set before calling S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Init(\+S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+I\+T\+\_\+\+G\+A\+M\+E\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R) You can update mappings after the system is initialized with \mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__gamecontroller_8h_a2bd404799b40e27d75d3699c866904cf}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Game\+Controller\+Mapping\+For\+G\+U\+I\+D()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__gamecontroller_8h_a62cb682b1c589135cd32cce381d403f8}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Game\+Controller\+Add\+Mapping()}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a5295df139727cd78a0663afb0b91010b}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a5295df139727cd78a0663afb0b91010b}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+B\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+B\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+B\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+B\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+B\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD}{SDL\_HINT\_GRAB\_KEYBOARD}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+B\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+B\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD\char`\"{}}



A variable controlling whether grabbing input grabs the keyboard. 

This variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ Grab will affect only the mouse \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ Grab will affect mouse and keyboard

By default S\+DL will not grab the keyboard so system shortcuts still work. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_abe9410e8b6809c9fdcb1f69e6894a2e8}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_abe9410e8b6809c9fdcb1f69e6894a2e8}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED}{SDL\_HINT\_IDLE\_TIMER\_DISABLED}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+I\+O\+S\+\_\+\+I\+D\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+E\+R\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED\char`\"{}}



A variable controlling whether the idle timer is disabled on i\+OS. 

When an i\+OS app does not receive touches for some time, the screen is dimmed automatically. For games where the accelerometer is the only input this is problematic. This functionality can be disabled by setting this hint.

As of S\+DL 2.\+0.\+4, \mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a17846c713066aa29a86e1be205a7fc3e}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Enable\+Screen\+Saver()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a68eb0d850934fa1c7ac12c30f2d56a84}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Disable\+Screen\+Saver()}} accomplish the same thing on i\+OS. They should be preferred over this hint.

This variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ Enable idle timer \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ Disable idle timer \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a17c7ae7e0cbbdb6a5049f559a58228ad}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a17c7ae7e0cbbdb6a5049f559a58228ad}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+E\+D\+I\+T\+I\+NG@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+E\+D\+I\+T\+I\+NG}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+E\+D\+I\+T\+I\+NG@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+E\+D\+I\+T\+I\+NG}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+E\+D\+I\+T\+I\+NG}{SDL\_HINT\_IME\_INTERNAL\_EDITING}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+E\+D\+I\+T\+I\+NG~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+I\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+N\+A\+L\+\_\+\+E\+D\+I\+T\+I\+NG\char`\"{}}



A variable to control whether certain I\+M\+Es should handle text editing internally instead of sending S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+T\+E\+X\+T\+E\+D\+I\+T\+I\+NG events. 

The variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+T\+E\+X\+T\+E\+D\+I\+T\+I\+NG events are sent, and it is the application\textquotesingle{}s responsibility to render the text from these events and differentiate it somehow from committed text. (default) \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ If supported by the I\+ME then S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+T\+E\+X\+T\+E\+D\+I\+T\+I\+NG events are not sent, and text that is being composed will be rendered in its own UI. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a7f03e5cd7f050a5e9304e3bc46586b06}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a7f03e5cd7f050a5e9304e3bc46586b06}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+O\+S\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+H\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+I\+C\+A\+T\+OR@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+O\+S\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+H\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+I\+C\+A\+T\+OR}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+O\+S\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+H\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+I\+C\+A\+T\+OR@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+O\+S\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+H\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+I\+C\+A\+T\+OR}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+O\+S\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+H\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+I\+C\+A\+T\+OR}{SDL\_HINT\_IOS\_HIDE\_HOME\_INDICATOR}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+I\+O\+S\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+H\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+I\+C\+A\+T\+OR~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+I\+O\+S\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+E\+\_\+\+H\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+D\+I\+C\+A\+T\+OR\char`\"{}}



A variable controlling whether the home indicator bar on i\+Phone X should be hidden. 

This variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ The indicator bar is not hidden (default for windowed applications) \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ The indicator bar is hidden and is shown when the screen is touched (useful for movie playback applications) \char`\"{}2\char`\"{} -\/ The indicator bar is dim and the first swipe makes it visible and the second swipe performs the \char`\"{}home\char`\"{} action (default for fullscreen applications) \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_ab343c91586c6b4789763e4a82b35de0b}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_ab343c91586c6b4789763e4a82b35de0b}} 
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+J\+O\+Y\+S\+T\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+J\+O\+Y\+S\+T\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+J\+O\+Y\+S\+T\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+J\+O\+Y\+S\+T\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+J\+O\+Y\+S\+T\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS}{SDL\_HINT\_JOYSTICK\_ALLOW\_BACKGROUND\_EVENTS}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+J\+O\+Y\+S\+T\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+J\+O\+Y\+S\+T\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+TS\char`\"{}}



A variable that lets you enable joystick (and gamecontroller) events even when your app is in the background. 

The variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ Disable joystick \& gamecontroller input events when the application is in the background. \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ Enable joystick \& gamecontroller input events when the application is in the background.

The default value is \char`\"{}0\char`\"{}. This hint may be set at any time. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a1b75df316decc7aae5bc31b0595c1b01}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a1b75df316decc7aae5bc31b0595c1b01}}

\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+PP@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+PP}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+PP}{SDL\_HINT\_MAC\_BACKGROUND\_APP}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+PP~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+\_\+\+B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+N\+D\+\_\+\+A\+PP\char`\"{}}



When set don\textquotesingle{}t force the S\+DL app to become a foreground process. 

This hint only applies to Mac OS X. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a63dd635fa195f590f645c1170f50968d}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a63dd635fa195f590f645c1170f50968d}}

\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+\_\+\+C\+T\+R\+L\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+E\+M\+U\+L\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+I\+G\+H\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+CK@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+\_\+\+C\+T\+R\+L\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+E\+M\+U\+L\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+I\+G\+H\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+CK}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+\_\+\+C\+T\+R\+L\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+E\+M\+U\+L\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+I\+G\+H\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+CK}{SDL\_HINT\_MAC\_CTRL\_CLICK\_EMULATE\_RIGHT\_CLICK}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+\_\+\+C\+T\+R\+L\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+E\+M\+U\+L\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+I\+G\+H\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+CK~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+M\+A\+C\+\_\+\+C\+T\+R\+L\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+C\+K\+\_\+\+E\+M\+U\+L\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+R\+I\+G\+H\+T\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+CK\char`\"{}}



A variable that determines whether ctrl+click should generate a right-\/click event on Mac. 

If present, holding ctrl while left clicking will generate a right click event when on Mac. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a59083735a2377046c2fc72eb0a3e855f}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a59083735a2377046c2fc72eb0a3e855f}}

\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+C\+U\+S\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+C\+K\+T\+H\+R\+O\+U\+GH@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+C\+U\+S\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+C\+K\+T\+H\+R\+O\+U\+GH}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+hints.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+C\+U\+S\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+C\+K\+T\+H\+R\+O\+U\+GH}{SDL\_HINT\_MOUSE\_FOCUS\_CLICKTHROUGH}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+C\+U\+S\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+C\+K\+T\+H\+R\+O\+U\+GH~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+C\+U\+S\+\_\+\+C\+L\+I\+C\+K\+T\+H\+R\+O\+U\+GH\char`\"{}}



Allow mouse click events when clicking to focus an S\+DL window. 

This variable can be set to the following values\+: \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} -\/ Ignore mouse clicks that activate a window \char`\"{}1\char`\"{} -\/ Generate events for mouse clicks that activate a window

By default S\+DL will ignore mouse clicks that activate a window \mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a1a5034b3e1f390aed827bd627ebdd555}\label{_s_d_l__hints_8h_a1a5034b3e1f390aed827bd627ebdd555}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+R\+M\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+LE~\char`\"{}S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+R\+M\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+P\+E\+E\+D\+\_\+\+S\+C\+A\+LE\char`\"{}}



A variable setting the speed scale for mouse motion, in floating point, when the mouse is not in relative mode.
